# Brainchild — Agent Context

*Working memory for coding agents. Human-readable roadmap: `docs/roadmap.md`.*
*Living document — update at the end of each session.*

---

## Working Style (follow for every step)

- One step at a time. Test and commit before moving on. Never batch steps.
- Before making any change: explain what you're about to do and why, in plain language.
- Smallest possible change. If a step can be broken down, do so.
- Don't touch anything out of scope. Note it, don't change it.
- Audience: technical product manager, not a senior engineer. Define terms when used.

---

## Current Status

**Session 159 (April 24, 2026) — Phase 14.10 wizard Google sign-in step shipped. One commit (`46057ae`), ~2.5h. Triggered by the prereq audit's natural follow-up: with browser_profile/auth_state.json now relocated to `~/.brainchild/`, slotting sign-in into the wizard was unblocked.**

- **Pre-implementation alignment (~7 questions).** Walked the user through detection mechanism (auth_state.json fast-path vs live profile probe), email display tradeoff, reset semantics, signin-completion polling, skip default, shared-vs-per-bot UX framing, and test approach. User redirected on placement: signin runs **last** in the wizard (after API keys, before reveal) — fits the "bot's ready, give it the keys" arc better than gating fighter-select. Then pushed back on "no email scrape" trade-off when "always offer reauth" was added — no email = blind reauth choice; flipped the trade-off to scrape email at sign-in time *once* and cache to `~/.brainchild/google_account.json`, so no scrape ever needed in the detect branch (free because the signin browser is already on a Google page when SID lands). Picked re-auth flow (b): `Logout → ServiceLogin` inside same persistent profile, no nuking the 1.1 GB profile.
- **Module shape — `pipeline/google_signin.py` (~230 lines).** `detect_google_session()` pure helper reads `auth_state.json` for `.google.com` SID (via inline `_auth_state_has_sid` mirroring `validate_auth_state` — can't import session.py without dragging in config and tripping the BRAINCHILD_BOT gate) and reads `google_account.json` for cached email. `_capture_email()` navigates live page to `myaccount.google.com` and extracts via aria-label selectors with regex fallback against `inner_text("body")`. `_launch_signin_flow()` opens visible Chrome via Playwright with `executable_path` pointed at real `Google Chrome.app` (not bundled Chrome-for-Testing — profile binary compatibility), polls cookie jar at 1s interval up to 5min for SID, then writes both artifacts. `run_signin_step()` wires the detect-or-launch UI: detect branch shows `✓ signed in as <email>` + `Sign in with a different account? [y/n] (n)`; first-time path warns, prompts `Sign in now? [y/n] (y)`, launches; skip emits clear consequence message ("your bot will prompt for sign-in on first run").
- **Path-constant promotion + regression guard.** `GOOGLE_ACCOUNT_FILE` added to `config.py` next to BROWSER_PROFILE_DIR/AUTH_STATE_FILE/ENV_FILE/DEBUG_DIR. `tests/test_path_resolution.py` extended: allow-list updated, anti-drift scanner picks it up automatically, new `test_google_signin_paths_canonical_across_modules` enforces three-way agreement between wizard's three inlined constants and config — same byte-exact divergence guard the existing ENV_FILE three-way test installs. 10 path tests (up from 9), all green.
- **Tests — `tests/test_wizard_signin.py` (11 cases).** detect-undetected (no files), detect-undetected (no SID), detect-detected (no email cache, legacy case), detect-detected (with email), malformed account JSON, missing email key, email without `@`, `_read_account_email` happy + missing path, `_EMAIL_RE` matches aria-label sample + no-false-positive on plain text. Live launch flow not unit-tested by design — Playwright persistent-context mocking is brittle, gets its smoke test in Phase 14.8's clean-mac live-QA.
- **Three live-QA fix loops (the interesting bit).** (1) `BRAINCHILD_BOT not set` — first wizard run died at module-import because `google_signin.py` did `from brainchild import config`. Same trap `setup.py` works around for `_ENV_FILE`. Fixed by inlining the three path constants + the `_auth_state_has_sid` helper. (2) `Target page... has been closed` on Playwright launch — bundled Chrome-for-Testing tried to open the persistent profile that was originally created by real `Google Chrome.app`; Chrome refuses cross-binary profile opens, browser process died on launch with `kill EPERM`. Fixed by passing `executable_path` to match `macos_adapter.py:512`. (3) Detect-branch prompt rendered as garbled `" continue with this account ·  sign in with a different account"` because Rich was eating `[enter]`/`[r]` brackets as color markup. Reframed the prompt as conventional `Sign in with a different account? [y/n] (n)` — git/brew/apt convention, default = continue with current.
- **User had a legacy `~/.brainchild/browser_profile/` from session 158's relocation but no `auth_state.json`** (session 158 only relocated, didn't seed the storage_state file). Walked the user through whether to add a one-time live-probe migration helper (would seed auth_state.json from the existing profile) vs ask them to re-auth once. User: "There are no legacy installs besides mine. We are pre-launch so fallback is way overkill. Don't do that. If we can't simply migrate to the new file structure I'm happy to re-auth." Picked re-auth — zero code, one-time cost on the user, profile preserved. After they sign in once, every future wizard run hits the fast-path detect branch.
- **Roadmap.** Phase 14.10 marked ✅ shipped session 159. Phase 14 total down from ~12h to ~10h. Execution-order line updated: 15.9 ✅ → 14.10 ✅ → **14.11 (next)** → 15.10 → ...
- **Carry-over unchanged.** GitHub `operator → brainchild` repo rename still deferred (blocks 14.5 install.sh). Session 155's Issue 3 (text-block-before-tool-call wiring in `pipeline/llm.py:295-308`) still open. Debug scratch files still untracked (`debug/admit_*.{html,png}`, `debug/post_admit_*.{html,png}`).
- **Exact next step**: Phase 14.11 — wizard MCP "context, not just tools" copy tweak (~20m). Pure copy change to `pipeline/setup.py`'s step-2 picker intro + per-server captions; reframe MCPs from a tool palette to "tools + context" so users understand they're also bringing in their working context (Linear backlog, GitHub repos, Gmail inbox, Calendar). Picker mechanics unchanged. After that: Phase 15.10 (pre-launch hardening: edge-case audit + claude top-10 use-case research + other-bot live-test checklist). **Session 158 (April 23, 2026) — path-resolution audit + regression guards. Three commits (`4777a66`, `1b6a74d`, `7fff5c1`), ~3h. Triggered by a user question about adding a Google-signin step to the setup wizard; the orthogonal prereq (browser profile being pinned at the repo root instead of `~/.brainchild/`) surfaced during architecture discussion and became the scope.**

- **Why the prereq fix came first.** User wanted a wizard Google-signin step. Initial planning surfaced that the Chrome profile currently resolves via `os.path.dirname(... __file__ ...)` walked up 4 levels from `macos_adapter.py` — dev-mode lands at repo root, installed-mode lands in `site-packages` (broken). User explicitly asked to resolve this rather than defer: "I would actually like to resolve this while we're here first and not defer."
- **Commit `4777a66` — browser artifacts relocation.** `config.BROWSER_PROFILE_DIR` and `AUTH_STATE_FILE` switched to `str(Path.home() / ".brainchild" / ...)`; `_BASE` walk-up in `macos_adapter.py` dropped; migration shim added to `__main__.py` (`_migrate_legacy_browser_artifacts`) that relocates the 1.1 GB profile on first startup. Live-QA confirmed Google session survived the move.
- **Commit `1b6a74d` — audit follow-up on three more bugs.** Explore-agent audit found: (a) `setup.py:_ENV_FILE = _ROOT / ".env"` wrote to `<repo>/.env` while `__main__._bootstrap_claude_imports` and `brainchild edit env` targeted `~/.brainchild/.env` — latent divergence, API keys silently landed where nothing looked. (b) `session.save_debug` dumped to `<repo>/debug/` via the same `_BASE` pattern. (c) Adapter chat-button-failure screenshots used CWD-relative `"debug/chat_btn_not_found.png"`. Fixed all three: added `config.ENV_FILE` and `config.DEBUG_DIR`; `load_dotenv()` given an explicit absolute path; migration shim extended to cover `.env` (rename `_migrate_legacy_browser_artifacts` → `_migrate_legacy_user_artifacts`); setup.py inlines the same path (can't import config pre-BRAINCHILD_BOT); session.py and both adapters route through `config.DEBUG_DIR`. User's live `.env` migrated cleanly (1064 bytes preserved, API keys load from new location).
- **Commit `7fff5c1` — regression guards.** User asked "how come unit tests didn't catch this?" Diagnosis: existing tests checked logic, not filesystem invariants. Added two layers to `tests/test_path_resolution.py`. Layer 1: `test_all_config_paths_rooted_under_home_or_tmp` enumerates every `*_DIR`/`*_FILE`/`*_PATH` attr on config, asserts absolute + under HOME/tmp/var; anti-drift scanner fails when a new path attr isn't in the allow-list (caught `BOT_DIR` during dev as intended). Layer 2: `test_env_file_canonical_across_modules` asserts byte-exact agreement between `config.ENV_FILE`, `setup._ENV_FILE`, and `_resolve_config_target('env')` — the exact session-158 divergence can't recur silently. Companion `test_debug_dir_canonical_across_modules` verifies session.py + both adapters reach `mod.config is config`. 9 tests in the file (up from 5).
- **Roadmap.** Phase 14.10 added (`~2h`, ⬜) — wizard Google-signin step, slot-zero before fighter-select, detect-or-launch shape, skippable with warning, shared profile across bots. The path relocation is its explicit prereq (called out in the entry). Phase 14 total bumped +2h.
- **Carry-over unchanged from session 157.** GitHub `operator → brainchild` repo rename still deferred (blocks 14.5 installer). Session 155's Issue 3 (text-block-before-tool-call wiring in `pipeline/llm.py:295-308`) still open. Debug scratch files (`debug/admit_*`, `debug/post_admit_*`) still untracked since session 151; two new `admit_keyboard_fail.{html,png}` files appeared this session too, also untracked.
- **Git identity.** Commits `4777a66`, `1b6a74d`, `7fff5c1` all carry `jojo@jojos-MacBook-Pro.local` — consistent with sessions 153–157. Flag if you want it normalized.

**Session 157 (April 23, 2026) — per-MCP tool-call timeouts + exponential heartbeat backoff. One commit (`104db4b`), ~1h. Triggered by a live-QA report: Claude Code delegation reported failure at 30s, but the requested landing page appeared seconds later.**

- **Diagnosis from `/tmp/brainchild.log` around 21:34–21:35.** Tool call ran 21:34:46.470 → 21:35:16.475 (exactly 30.0s) then logged `Tool 'delegate_to_claude_code' failed: ` with nothing after the colon. Fingerprint of a `concurrent.futures.TimeoutError` (stringifies to `""`) and a 30-second limit nobody configured. Found it in `pipeline/mcp_client.py:503` — `_ServerHandle.call_tool` had `timeout=30` hardcoded as a default parameter. The bot's outer heartbeat loop was reading the `tool_timeout_seconds: 600` override from config, but that value never reached the inner `future.result(timeout=...)` call. Two uncoordinated stopwatches; the tighter one won. Meanwhile the asyncio task kept running, the `claude -p` subprocess finished naturally, and the user saw the "failure" plus the completed work.
- **Architecture conversation.** Walked the user through the two-stopwatches history plainly (outer drives heartbeats; inner is a defensive ceiling on the blocking call), then proposed "inner = outer + 5s safety margin." User pushed back: per-MCP timeouts make sense because different MCPs enable different task durations (Claude Code = minutes, Linear = seconds), and we should have one source of truth, not two. Agreed — collapsed to: MCP layer owns the timeout, chat_runner only drives heartbeats. The outer loop doesn't disappear (it has to keep posting "Still working"), but it loses its deadline.
- **"Why can't the bot multi-task?" answered.** Two reasons: (a) chat loop is single-threaded serial today — when it dispatches a tool call, it blocks instead of continuing to poll; (b) Anthropic tool-use API requires `tool_use` → `tool_result` to be consecutive in the conversation, no user turn between them. Walked through three options (ambient acknowledgement, parallel side-chat threads, cancel-and-restart) with cost estimates. User picked A (timeout fix only this session) and left the side-chat lifts explicitly deferred.
- **Shipped — `104db4b`.** `config.DEFAULT_TOOL_TIMEOUTS` map added with ship-level defaults per MCP (claude-code=600, playwright=300, figma=90, github/salesforce=60, notion=45, linear/sentry/slack/calendar/gmail/drive=30). `config.TOOL_HEARTBEAT_MAX_SECONDS=60` added for the exponential cap. `mcp_client._effective_timeout_for` walks override → default map → global fallback; `_ServerHandle.call_tool` now takes a required `timeout`, best-effort cancels the underlying task on expiry (`future.cancel()`), and raises an informative `MCPToolError` that tells the LLM which knob to turn. `chat_runner._execute_and_respond` lost its deadline/`timed_out` branch entirely — the existing error-handler branch relays MCP timeouts verbatim. Heartbeat is now `8s → 16s → 32s → 60s cap`. Tests rewritten (`test_912_tool_timeout.py`) to match the new contract, new `test_heartbeat_interval_backs_off` locks in exponential behavior, new `test_effective_timeout_precedence` in `test_mcp_client_units.py`. Full sweep green.
- **Docs.** `agents/README.md` `tool_timeout_seconds` table row updated. Two stale "global 60s TOOL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS for this MCP only" comments in bundled claude/engineer configs rewritten.
- **Expected live-QA behavior change.** Claude Code delegation now gets the full 600s the config says it should. Log line at MCP execute will show `timeout=600s` so you can sanity-check. Heartbeats on a long delegation: 8s, 24s, 56s, 116s, 176s, 236s… — tight reassurance early, sparse as it goes long. No more 8-second-forever stream.
- **Deferred (explicit this session).** (a) Ambient acknowledgement — keep chat loop polling during tool call so side messages get a "still finishing, will answer after" reply (~half day). (b) Full parallel side-chat threads or cancel-and-restart. User said disregard on the natural-language path-resolution option surfaced from the same live-QA log.
- **Exact next step**: live-QA the timeout fix in a real Meet. Confirm Claude Code delegations now complete cleanly with no false failure and heartbeats back off as expected. After verification: Phase 14.5 `install.sh` (~2h, still blocked on GitHub `operator → brainchild` repo rename). Quick-hop alt if still blocked: **14.7 uninstall docs (~10m)** or session 155's open **Issue 3 — text-block-before-tool-call wiring in `pipeline/llm.py:295-308`** (~30–45m, genuine chat-feel win).
- **Budget**: ~1h burned on session 157. MVP envelope: ~16.5–18.5h remaining. Launch target Apr 28–30 aspirational / May 1–2 acceptable.

**Session 156 (April 23, 2026) — config discoverability (`brainchild edit` + `brainchild where`) and a long architecture conversation. One commit (`01b0868`), ~45 min of code + ~45 min of discussion + bundled-config comment cleanup.**

- **Live-QA trigger — "I said something aloud, bot didn't know."** User had captions_enabled flipped to `true` in the *bundled* `src/brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml` but was running against `~/.brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml` which still had `captions_enabled: false`. Root caused by reading `/tmp/brainchild.log`: no `caption bridge exposed` / `caption: [Jojo] …` lines → the caption pipeline was never wired on boot. Fixed the user's runtime copy (`~/.brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml` → `true`) to unblock QA, then fixed the bundled config's stale comment ("Captions off by default…") to match the actual value (`true`) — that comment edit was rolled into session 155's `87255e0`, not a separate session 156 commit.
- **Architecture discussion — two-dir split (`src/brainchild/agents/` bundled vs `~/.brainchild/agents/` user).** User challenged whether the split is overengineered. Made the case for it: package installs are immutable/read-only on locked-down systems, upgrades need to add new bundled agents without destroying user customizations, multi-user machines need per-home configs, and this is the standard template-plus-overlay pattern (`/etc/gitconfig` + `~/.gitconfig`, VS Code bundled vs user extensions, `~/.claude/` overlay). The dev-mode confusion is real but is a dev-mode artifact (the bundled dir is normally buried under `.venv/lib/python3.x/site-packages/` and invisible to end users). The actual gaps are (a) no `brainchild setup --sync-bundled` to propagate bundled-config edits to existing installs, and (b) no dev-mode symlink affordance so repo-edits of bundled configs hit runtime immediately.
- **Scope discussion — should agents be repo-proximal (per-project) instead of per-user?** No. Brainchild is user-scoped by nature: the bot's identity (personality, MCPs, skills) travels with the human, not with whatever repo tab they have open. Compare Claude Code (repo-scoped: reads CLAUDE.md, edits that repo's files) vs brainchild (runs in a browser, joins a Meet — cwd is irrelevant). The install + run-from-anywhere UX is intended. Per-project overrides are a narrow post-MVP story at best.
- **Shipped — `brainchild edit` + `brainchild where` (`01b0868`).** ~55 lines in `src/brainchild/__main__.py`. `edit <bot|.env>` opens the file in `$VISUAL`/`$EDITOR`/`vi` (multi-word editors via `shlex.split` so `EDITOR="code --wait"` works); `where <bot|.env>` prints the absolute path for shell composition (`code $(brainchild where claude)`, `open -R $(brainchild where claude)`). Accepts `.env` or bare `env` as the env-file token. Centralized `_resolve_config_target` so both give identical error shapes on unknown targets. Wired into `main()` dispatch and both the top-of-file docstring and `_print_usage`. Smoke-tested: happy path (all four bots + `.env` + `env`), missing file (rc=1, clean error), unknown target (rc=2, usage), no-arg (rc=2, usage).
- **Deferred (~10m each, offered).** (a) Append a "for further tweaks, run `brainchild edit <name>`" line to the wizard reveal screen — closes the long-tail discoverability loop at the moment of first config-touch. (b) Draft `brainchild setup --sync-bundled` — per-key diff of bundled vs user with accept/skip prompts. Both parked for user decision.
- **Incidental finding.** User's `~/.brainchild/.env` doesn't exist on this machine — they've been running with shell-exported env vars. The Phase 14.5 installer will seed an empty `.env` at first install; worth keeping in mind that the wizard's env-appending code paths (e.g., `append_env_placeholders` in `claude_code_import.py`) assume the file is writeable and may silently create it on first append.
- **Exact next step**: Phase 14.5 `install.sh` (~2h), still blocked on GitHub `operator → brainchild` repo rename. Quick-hop alt if still blocked: **14.7 uninstall docs (~10m)**. Issue 3 from session 155 (text-block-before-tool-call wiring in `pipeline/llm.py:295-308`) also still open, ~30–45 min — genuine chat-feel win when the user returns to that work.
- **Budget**: ~45 min burned on session 156 subcommand ship. MVP envelope unchanged. Launch target Apr 28–30 aspirational / May 1–2 acceptable.

**Session 155 (April 23, 2026) — live-QA fixes for the claude bundled agent. One commit (`87255e0`), ~1h. Triggered by an interactive `brainchild run claude` test in a real Meet — three independent issues surfaced in one user turn, plus an intro-timing bug from a follow-up QA pass.**

- **Issue 1 — replies way too long, no length cap firing.** Root cause: `~/.brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml` had `personality: ''` and `ground_rules: ''` — both wiped to empty strings. The bundled defaults (terse-precise-plan-first personality + 1–3-sentences rule + delegation rules) never reached the model on this run. Diagnosed back to `setup.py::_step4_system_prompt` line 806–808: any `brainchild setup` run that hit step 4 with empty input would `state.bot_cfg["personality"] = ""; state.bot_cfg["ground_rules"] = ""` — overwriting the preset's defaults with empty strings instead of preserving them. The hint copy ("Leave empty to skip") matched the buggy behavior, not the desired behavior.
- **Issue 2 — bot improvising `<search_web>` XML inline as text.** Two contributing causes: (a) no `web_search` MCP is exposed to the model — the Claude Code CLI has `WebSearch` built in but it's a CLI-internal tool, not an MCP we surface; (b) without personality/ground_rules, no framing told the model to refuse rather than fake. Fixed by restoring defaults plus a new ground-rule line ("Never write tool calls as text… offer to delegate to Claude Code") AND a personality addition ("Claude Code is your universal escape hatch: anything you can't do directly in chat — web search, file reads, code work, running commands — you can delegate to a sandboxed Claude Code worktree, which has the full Claude Code toolkit (WebSearch, WebFetch, Bash, Read/Edit/Write) inside it"). Both edits applied to BOTH the user's installed copy AND the bundled config so future seeds carry them.
- **Issue 3 — pre-tool-call ack / message-splitting UX.** Investigated. Anthropic's API returns BOTH a text block AND a tool_use block in the same response when the model wants to acknowledge before calling — `pipeline/llm.py:295-308` currently keeps only the tool_call and drops the text on the floor. Fix would be to send the text block first as a "let me check…" buffer, then fall through to the confirmation/execute path. Zero added latency, zero extra API calls. **Not implemented this session** — user wanted to verify the long-reply fix in live QA before piling on a second change. This is the next obvious lever for the chat-feel work; ~30–45 min.
- **Issue 4 (follow-up QA) — `brainchild run claude` (no URL) appears to skip the intro.** Investigated via /tmp/brainchild.log. Both paths actually post the intro — log shows `MacOSAdapter: chat sent: "I'm Claude Code…"` ~3s after bot joins in both meet.new and URL paths. The visibility difference is on the user's end: in meet.new mode, `webbrowser.open(url)` pops the user's default browser, but the user is still on Meet's pre-join screen / opening the chat panel when the bot posts the intro, AND Meet only shows chat messages received after you've opened the chat panel. So the bot effectively ghosts on first contact in meet.new mode. Fix: `chat_runner.py:209-219` now gates the intro post on `saw_others` (at least one other participant detected in the meeting). Bot waits for a human to actually appear before introducing itself. URL-given path with humans already in meeting is unchanged (`saw_others` flips on first participant check).
- **Test delta.** Added `test_intro_waits_for_human_in_empty_room` to `tests/test_chat_runner_gaps.py` — uses `participant_counts=[1, 1, 2]` to assert the intro only posts after the bump to 2. All 28 chat_runner tests green. Existing intro tests still work because `make_runner()` defaults to `participant_counts=2`.
- **Verification.** Composed `SYSTEM_PROMPT` for the claude bot now contains all three target rules (`'1–3 sentences' in SYSTEM_PROMPT == True`, `'escape hatch' in SYSTEM_PROMPT == True`, `'Never write tool calls' in SYSTEM_PROMPT == True`). Length: 2636 chars total. Re-test in a live Meet should produce a terser reply that either delegates web-search work or says it can't do it directly.
- **Exact next step**: re-test the claude bot in a live Meet — confirm reply length drops, confirm the intro lands when you (the human) join the popped browser. If both clean, the chat-feel work continues with **Issue 3 (text-block-before-tool-call wiring in `pipeline/llm.py:295-308`)** before resuming the planned **Phase 14.5 install.sh**.
- **Budget**: ~1h burned on session 155 reactive QA work. MVP envelope unchanged.

**Session 154 (April 23, 2026) — MCP boot-path hardening + new static bootability test. Three commits (`b21d7fc`, `130831c`, `ddfb3d7`), ~1h. Unplanned work triggered by a live `brainchild run claude` failure.**

- **Trigger.** User ran `brainchild run claude` and got `can't open file '/Users/jojo/Desktop/operator/agents/engineer/claude_code.py': [Errno 2] No such file or directory`. The bundled `claude-code` MCP's args were `python agents/engineer/claude_code.py` — a relative path rotted by the src-layout packaging move. File now lives at `src/brainchild/agents/engineer/claude_code.py`; CWD at MCP-server spawn time is the user's invocation dir (repo root today via the launcher's `cd`, but won't be under `uv tool install`).
- **Fix 1 — `b21d7fc` claude-code MCP args: script path → module invocation.** Flipped all four bundled agents (`claude/engineer/pm/designer`) from `["agents/engineer/claude_code.py"]` to `["-m", "brainchild.agents.engineer.claude_code"]`. Namespace-package import verified (no `__init__.py` needed under PEP 420). Works from any CWD in both dev and post-install.
- **Fix 2 — `130831c` github MCP command: relative path → bare name on PATH.** Audit surfaced the same bug class: `./github-mcp-server` across all four bundled agents. Only engineer has it `enabled: true` by default; others are dormant but still on the shipping contract. Swapped to bare `"github-mcp-server"` (PATH lookup). Symlinked `/Users/jojo/Desktop/operator/github-mcp-server → ~/.local/bin/` for immediate local use; Phase 14.5's `install.sh` takes ownership long-term. Preserved the full 41-tool Go-binary surface (npm `@modelcontextprotocol/server-github` remains ruled out per session-57 commit `52a65a8` — broken `search_code` auth, documented in `docs/mcp-pressure-test.md:193`).
- **User-installed copies patched out-of-band.** Five `~/.brainchild/agents/{claude,engineer,pm,designer,testbot}/config.yaml` files updated for both bugs so the current install works without re-seeding. These live outside git and aren't part of any commit.
- **New test — `ddfb3d7` `tests/test_bundled_mcps_bootable_static.py` (227 lines, 3 tests).** Walks every `src/brainchild/agents/*/config.yaml` and every MCP block (ENABLED AND DISABLED — shipping the definition implies boot must work if the wizard flips it on). Rules: bare command → `shutil.which`; `python -m <mod>` → `importlib.util.find_spec`; `python <script>` → absolute path exists; absolute command → exists+executable; relative path of any flavor → FAIL with a message that names `uv tool install` as the reason. Third test warns (doesn't fail) on `@latest` npx entries — surfaced 12 warnings matching the 15.7.5 pressure-test punch list (calendar/salesforce/slack × 4 agents). Proved to catch both today's bugs via direct calls to `_classify_command`.
- **Tier 2 dynamic bootability** (spawn each MCP, call `initialize()` + `list_tools()`, kill after 5s) deferred — needs credential fixtures for auth-required servers; belongs in deferred-live-tests until then.
- **Exact next step**: Phase 14.5 `install.sh` (~2h), still blocked on the GitHub `operator → brainchild` repo rename. Quick-hop: 14.7 uninstall docs (~10m). Nothing in session 154 moves the 14.5 framing.
- **Budget**: ~1h burned on session 154 (unplanned). MVP envelope unchanged — this was reactive work on a live bug, not roadmap burn. Launch target Apr 28–30 aspirational, May 1–2 acceptable.

**Uncommitted at session end (user's in-flight edits, not session work):** `src/brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml` carries three user-authored edits on top of the session-154 github fix — `captions_enabled: true`, a "never fabricate tool calls" ground-rule, a "Claude Code as universal escape hatch" personality paragraph. `src/brainchild/pipeline/setup.py` has a separate pre-session modification, untouched this session. Both deserve commit messages the user authors themselves.

**Session 153 (April 23, 2026) — setup-wizard UX polish. One commit (`777add3`), ~1h. No phase assignment — this is pre-launch polish on top of the 15.5.5/15.11 wizard surface.**

- **Scope.** User ran through `brainchild setup` interactively and called out a stream of seven UI issues in a single turn, then four more across the session. Everything landed surgically in `build_card.py` / `picker.py` / `setup.py` + one test update. No roadmap phase invented; this is polish, not a named deliverable.
- **Build card (`src/brainchild/pipeline/build_card.py`).** Root cause of "the card expands with each selection" was Rich's `Panel(width=N)` default of `expand=False`, which lets the panel shrink to content (so short taglines rendered a narrower card than long ones) AND can stretch when inside a `Table.grid` cell. Fix: `expand=True` + `width=width` is absolute — the panel is always exactly N cells. Added terminal-aware sizing via `width_for(console, left_min=26, padding=8) → clamp(MIN_WIDTH=28, DEFAULT_WIDTH=40, console.size.width - 34)` so narrow terminals shrink the card instead of clipping its right border. Threaded `width` through `_compose_body(..., inner=...)` so every internal wrap calc honors the passed width. Each MCP and skill now gets its own row via shared `_render_list(label, glyph, items)` helper with hanging indent; both lists cap at `MAX_LIST_ITEMS=5` with a dim `+N more` overflow marker (regex-wrapped in `[dim]...[/dim]` AFTER padding so cell-length math stays correct). "power-ups" label renamed to "MCPs" (both labels still padded to 12 cells so `⚡` and `★` glyphs align vertically). Lightning bolts recolored `bold blue` → `bold magenta`.
- **Picker (`src/brainchild/pipeline/picker.py`).** Added `_viewport(cursor, total, max_visible)` that returns the half-open slice of choice indices to render, centering the cursor and clamping at bounds. `_render_rows` now accepts `max_visible` and emits `↑ N more above` / `↓ N more below` dim markers when clipped. `select_many` computes `max_visible = max(3, (console.size.height - 10) // rows_per_choice)` with `rows_per_choice=2` when any sublabel is present (label + sublabel = 2 rows each). `_layout` accepts `right_pane_width` and `select_one` computes it from `console.size.width` the same way `build_card.width_for` does (so step 1's fighter-select preview panel shrinks proportionally and matches the build card).
- **Setup wizard (`src/brainchild/pipeline/setup.py`).** Several independent edits: (1) Removed the `[dim]editing agents/claude/ in place[/dim]` flash in `_edit_preset`. (2) `_OFFICIAL_MCPS` gained `playwright`, `salesforce`, `sentry` (their MCP servers are first-party from Microsoft / Salesforce Inc. / Sentry Inc.). Deliberately left off: `calendar` (community `@cocal` fork, not Google's own), `slack` (archived `@modelcontextprotocol/server-slack` reference server, not Slack Inc.). (3) `_render_skill_picker` dropped the `[shared library]` / `[from ~/...]` source tag from sublabels; truncation budget is now dynamic — `max(24, console.size.width - card_w - 8 - 6 - 2)` where `card_w = build_card.width_for(console)` — so the description never wraps to a second line, on any terminal width. Added `_truncate(text, limit)` helper. (4) `_prompt_with_hint` gained `dim=False` opt-out; the "Add an external skills folder" block passes `dim=False` so the instructional copy renders white (user-facing instruction, not dim placeholder hint). (5) `_auto_import_claude_setup` now flips bundled blocks' `enabled=true` when the user has that MCP configured in Claude Code (previously a no-op on name collision — the bundled scaffold stayed default-off even when the user had the server set up; felt like a bug to the user). New-block path unchanged (imports arrive with `enabled: True` from `claude_code_import`). Pre-check fix: only skills with `src != "shared library"` get added to `state.enabled_skill_names` — bundled shared-library skills stay off by default. Rationale: the claude agent's identity is "your Claude Code setup is the toolkit"; pre-selecting bundled Brainchild skills (pr-review, release-notes, etc.) dilutes that. Import summary renders separate counts for "imported", "enabled from your Claude Code setup", and "skills pre-selected". (6) `_reveal` re-ordered so the build card sits between "All set" and the config-path + run-command lines — card is the hero artifact, the instructions are the call-to-action below it.
- **Claude preset tagline rewritten** — `src/brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml`: "Claude Code, in your meeting — sandboxed with all your skills and MCP's loaded in" (was "plan-first, sandboxed, ready to delegate"). User explicitly specified this copy.
- **`_ensure_user_agents` sync is additive** — confirmed mid-session when the user reported the new tagline not appearing in step 1. Root cause: `~/.brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml` was seeded on a prior run with the old tagline, and the session-151 per-bot-sync only copies a bundled agent if it doesn't already exist (intentional so user customizations aren't stomped). Solution used here: deleted all four installed agent dirs (user explicitly authorized — "they're all for testing"); next `brainchild` invocation will re-seed from bundled sources. Flagged in conversation as a potential Phase 14.x `--sync-bundled` flag, not urgent.
- **Test delta.** One test touched: `tests/test_setup.py::test_build_card_empty_bullets_show_placeholder` — (a) `_compose_body` signature gained required `inner=` kwarg, so added `inner=build_card.DEFAULT_WIDTH - 2`; (b) `power-ups:` → `MCPs:` asserted label literal updated. All 13 setup tests + 30 claude_code_import tests green.
- **Exact next step**: Phase 14.5 `install.sh` (~2h), still blocked on the GitHub `operator → brainchild` repo rename. No code change from this session affects the 14.5 framing. Alternative quick-hop: 14.7 uninstall docs (~10m).
- **Budget**: ~1h burned on session 153 polish. MVP budget unchanged envelope-wise — this was user-priority work, not roadmap work. Launch target Apr 28–30 aspirational, May 1–2 acceptable.

**Session 151 (April 22, 2026) — Phase 15.9 `claude` bundled agent shipped. Two commits, ~4h.**

- **Scope and intent.** User asked to add a fourth bundled agent called `claude` — "Claude Code in your meeting." Defining trait: auto-inherit the user's existing Claude Code setup so power users don't re-configure everything. Original ask was post-MVP v1.1 (~5h estimate); user pulled it into this session. Explicit no-new-skills cut — ship the agent + auto-import machinery, skills deferred. `/slash-command` audit ran as a preliminary step (see "Rejected scope" below).
- **Five sub-steps in one session, tracked live with TaskCreate.** (15.9.0) agent scaffold at `src/brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml` copied from PM baseline; claude-code MCP enabled with beefed-up "built by Brainchild, sandboxed worktree" description + 600s tool timeout; other 9 MCPs scaffolded disabled for auto-import to flip on; trigger `@claude`, captions off (chat-directed delegation, not ambient). (15.9.1) `_ensure_user_agents()` in `__main__.py` changed from "copy bundled only if user dir empty" to per-bot sync — existing users get `claude` on next run without blowing away their agents dir; tradeoff documented (deliberately-deleted bundled bot reappears). (15.9.2) new `pipeline/claude_code_import.py` (~265 lines): public `claude_code_installed_and_logged_in()` wraps `readiness._probe_claude_code`; three discovery sources merged via `discover_all_mcps()` — `~/.claude.json#mcpServers` + `claude mcp list` subprocess (regex-parsed, 10s timeout, degrades to empty on format drift) + `~/.claude/skills/` + `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`. HTTP/SSE entries auto-wrap via `mcp-remote@0.1.38` with `auth: oauth` + `auth_url` so existing 15.7.3 cache-path check + `brainchild auth <name>` flow work unchanged on imports. `append_env_placeholders` idempotent. 32 unit tests in `tests/test_claude_code_import.py` — all green. (15.9.3) four surgical wizard hooks in `pipeline/setup.py`: step 1 blocks claude preset selection when CLI missing ("option b" — show but hint-and-recurse); `_edit_preset("claude")` invokes new `_auto_import_claude_setup(state)` which merges imports into `state.bot_cfg` (dedup by name — user curation wins); step 2 end appends env placeholders for newly-enabled imports; step 3 surfaces imported skills summary; step 4 offers optional CLAUDE.md → ground_rules append. (15.9.4) two hooks in `__main__.py::_run_bot`: hard-fail gate (exit 2 + clean stderr when CLI not ready) and idempotent `_bootstrap_claude_imports()` first-run auto-import (marker `_claude_import_done: true` prevents re-running the ~3s `claude mcp list` shell-out on subsequent boots). (15.9.5) docs sync: roadmap Phase 15.9 block, 4 new deferred-live-tests entries, CLAUDE.md paragraph, handoff.
- **Key implementation finding — `claude mcp list` is the authoritative source for hosted connectors.** See Hard Won Knowledge below. `~/.claude.json#mcpServers` was the obvious candidate but is empty for users who configure MCPs via claude.ai account connectors (Gmail / Drive / Calendar / Linear — most power users). Text-parsing the CLI output is the only way to reach them.
- **Clean commit split.** `9c0283b` code (5 files, +1458/-11): agent + import module + tests + setup.py wizard hooks + `__main__.py` sync-refactor + hard-fail + bootstrap. `1d11084` docs (4 files, +98/-4): roadmap + deferred-live-tests + handoff + CLAUDE.md. Both carry the auto-identity `jojo@jojos-MacBook-Pro.local` — consistent with prior session commits.
- **Live end-to-end verification on author's machine.** `_edit_preset("claude")` against actual Claude Code install discovered 4 hosted MCPs (Gmail / Drive / Calendar / Linear) + 2 user skills (begin-session / end-session). `_bootstrap_claude_imports` end-to-end against throwaway home: 10 → 14 MCPs after first call, marker set, second call no-op (idempotent). Hard-fail mock test confirms exit 2 + clean stderr. 80+ regressions green across 4 adjacent suites.
- **Rejected scope — five translated slash-command skills.** Session-151 `/` audit inventoried all 80 Claude Code built-in slash commands against Brainchild's Meet-chat context. Shortlist: `/plan` → plan, `/recap` → meeting-recap, `/security-review` → security-review, `/bug` → file-bug, `/simplify` → code-cleanup. User deferred post-launch per "ship the agent, skills later." If resurrected as Phase 15.9.6, estimated ~2h for the five-skill pack. Audit findings captured in chat mid-session, not persisted to a doc because scope was deliberately cut.
- **Known limitation — PyYAML comment-drop.** `_bootstrap_claude_imports` does YAML round-trip on first write; comments in `~/.brainchild/agents/claude/config.yaml` are lost. Matches the existing `_step7_write` wizard behavior (same limitation already logged in Hard Won Knowledge). Documented in handoff + deferred-live-tests so future sessions don't re-discover.
- **Exact next step**: Phase 14.5 `install.sh` (~2h), still blocked on GitHub `operator → brainchild` repo rename for the `uv tool install git+...` URL. Alternative quick-hop: 14.7 uninstall docs (~10m, README-only).

**Session 150 (April 22, 2026) — Phase 15.8.1 CLI verb rename shipped. One commit, ~1h.**

- **Entered post-compact from session 149** with 15.8.0 audit already captured in `docs/roadmap.md`. User asked what pre-launch items could run async to 15.7.5/15.7.6 happening in another session; landed on **15.8.1 rename** (no collision — 15.7.5/6 touch agent `config.yaml` + new skill files; 15.8.1 touches `__main__.py` / README-family / `setup.py` / `config.py` / tests).
- **21 documented changes landed atomically across 7 files** per the 15.8.0 inventory: `src/brainchild/__main__.py` (7 hits), `README.md` (2), `CLAUDE.md` (3), `src/brainchild/agents/README.md` (2), per-agent READMEs pm/engineer/designer (6), `pipeline/setup.py` (2), `config.py` (1). Every `brainchild <name>` / `brainchild {name}` / `brainchild {bot}` form flipped to `brainchild run ...`.
- **Audit missed 2 tests.** `tests/test_entry_cli.py` had `test_main_known_bot_dispatches_to_run_bot` + `test_main_unknown_bot_returns_2` exercising the bare form — 15.8.0's zero-hit-tests claim was wrong; the audit scanned for string literals but missed positional-argv test shapes like `["pm", "<url>"]`. Fixed in-commit: renamed the first to `test_main_run_known_bot_dispatches_to_run_bot` with `["run", "pm", "<url>"]`, added three new tests (`test_main_bare_known_bot_rejected_with_run_hint`, `test_main_run_without_name_returns_2`, `test_main_run_unknown_bot_returns_2`). Updates the runner list too.
- **Dispatcher shape.** Added `run` branch that requires a name (usage + exit 2 if missing) and validates it against `_available_bots()` (exit 2 + usage otherwise). Distinct **bare-known-bot** branch prints a pointed hint (``Run agents via `brainchild run pm`. Bare `brainchild pm` is no longer supported.``) and exits 2 — gives truly-unknown args the generic "Unknown bot or subcommand" message, but a familiar bot name gets a self-documenting pointer. No dual-accept. `_print_usage` collapsed the two-form lines into one `brainchild run <name> [url]` line with "auto-opens one if no url" inline so the new surface stays compact.
- **Minor 14.7 scope revision noticed in-session** — roadmap.md already had a pre-existing edit narrowing 14.7 from a dedicated `brainchild uninstall` subcommand (~30m) to three lines in the README + natural `uv tool uninstall` (~10m). Rationale baked into that row: `uv tool install`-style CLIs don't ship their own uninstallers (pipx/cargo/npm all defer to the package manager); Homebrew/nvm/Ollama wrappers exist because they touch system locations, we don't. Left as-is; not a session-150 change.
- **Verification.** 26/26 `tests/test_entry_cli.py` green (up from 23 before the three added cases). `tests/test_setup.py` green (reveal copy still renders — wizard tests mock dispatch, don't assert on the exact line). `python -m brainchild` emits the new usage string; `python -m brainchild pm` emits the pointed hint and exits 2.
- **Exact next step**: 14.5 `install.sh` after 15.7.5 + 15.7.6 close (those are running async in another session). 14.5 still blocks on the GitHub repo rename `operator → brainchild` for the `uv tool install git+https://...` URL — unchanged from sessions 146+. Alternative immediate pickup: 14.7 uninstall docs (~10m) — three README lines, zero dependencies.
- **Budget**: 15.8 came in at ~1h vs the 1.5h estimate (~30m shaved). MVP budget: ~25.75–27.75h remaining.

**Session 149 async continuation (April 22, 2026) — Phase 15.7.5 + 15.7.6 shipped. Two commits, ~2h.**

- **Kicked off while session 150 was driving 15.8.1 in parallel.** User asked what pre-launch step could run async that didn't depend on in-flight 15.7.4.5; agreed on 15.7.5 (new-MCP scaffolding) + 15.7.6 (six skills) as a two-commit unit since both are YAML/markdown, no Python changes, and both stay clear of 15.8.1's `__main__.py` / README-family surface. Verified 15.7.4 already committed as `0432bad`; 15.7.4.5 committed mid-session as `a97d4fc`; doc sync as `8421b6a`. Working tree surveyed for collision risk (low — 15.8.1 touches Python, 15.7.5/6 touch config YAML + new skill files).
- **15.7.5 new-MCP scaffolding (commit `5453080`, +489/-2).** Dispatched a general-purpose research agent to get canonical package names / auth shapes for the five new servers (calendar, playwright, salesforce, sentry, slack) — findings informed the five YAML blocks. Inserted alphabetically in all three agent configs (`calendar` before `claude-code`; `playwright`/`salesforce`/`sentry`/`slack` after `notion`). Per-server details: calendar (@cocal/google-calendar-mcp, `auth: env` via `GOOGLE_OAUTH_CREDENTIALS` as an absolute path to a local credentials.json downloaded from Google Cloud Console — the server handles OAuth refresh internally, so the env var is a file path not a token); playwright (@playwright/mcp@0.0.70, no auth, no env — browser state persists in the platform cache dir); salesforce (@salesforce/mcp, `env: {}` with auth delegated to `sf` CLI's local cache from `sf org login web`); sentry (hosted remote MCP via `mcp-remote@0.1.38` against `https://mcp.sentry.dev/mcp`, OAuth via DCR — identical pattern to Linear's 15.7.3 config); slack (@modelcontextprotocol/server-slack with `SLACK_BOT_TOKEN`/`SLACK_TEAM_ID`). Enablement per session-147 rule: PM flipped github true→false and added calendar enabled:true; Engineer added sentry enabled:true (kept claude-code + github); Designer flipped linear true→false (kept figma only). slack/salesforce/playwright scaffolded `enabled: false` on all three. Each block declares `auth` / `credentials_url` / `env` / `read_tools` (5–6 items, read-only auto-execute allowlist) / `confirm_tools` / `hints`. Hints are grounded in each server's known quirks (calendar RFC3339 timestamps + get-freebusy over inferred conflicts; playwright snapshots-over-screenshots + confirm-before-navigate; salesforce PascalCase objects + describe-before-guess; sentry org/project scoping + query syntax literal-copy; slack channel-IDs not names + `<@U...>` user pings). **Pin strategy**: three new entries (calendar / salesforce / slack) ship `@latest` with an inline "pin after pressure-testing" comment rather than fake a version I couldn't confirm — playwright@0.0.70 and mcp-remote@0.1.38 are real pinned. Each pin TODO captured in the deferred-live-tests entry.
- **Zero Python changes required.** 15.7.1's `_resolve_env_vars` already regex-scans `${VAR}` over any env dict; 15.7.3's `oauth_cache_exists` already works on any `auth: oauth` server; 15.7.4's `report_mcp_readiness` is generic over both. New blocks flow through without code edits. Verified by loading each config via `yaml.safe_load` directly (config.py reads from `~/.brainchild/agents/` which is user-owned, so the bundled `src/brainchild/agents/*/config.yaml` can only be validated via direct YAML parse — intentional, matches session-147 insulation).
- **Salesforce readiness UX gap flagged.** With `env: {}` and `auth: env`, `report_mcp_readiness` reports ✓ for a salesforce block even when `sf` CLI isn't logged in — the real auth lives in the CLI's local cache, not an env var. Tools spawn but calls fail. Two resolutions possible post-launch: (a) add a prereq probe analogous to claude-code's 15.7.4 pattern (shutil.which("sf") + `sf org list --json`), (b) accept the gap and let the mid-meeting banner catch it. Flagged in the deferred-live-tests entry; no action taken in 15.7.5 proper.
- **Pressure-test matrix** parked in `docs/deferred-live-tests.md` under a new Phase 15.7.5 section — one entry per MCP with setup, verify steps, and pin-pending TODOs where applicable. Blanket pass criterion: tools appear in `get_openai_tools()` + at least one read tool returns a real payload + no `startup_failures` entry for the server. User installs at `~/.brainchild/agents/` intentionally unchanged (narrower bundle defaults apply to fresh installs and post-`rm -rf ~/.brainchild/agents/` reseed only). Regression: 20/20 test_1574_readiness + 28/28 test_mcp_client + 13/13 test_1571_error_classification + 10/10 test_1573_oauth_cache_check + chat_hardening all green.
- **15.7.6 six new skills (commit `4986743`, +394/-2).** Each SKILL.md follows the existing frontmatter + Shape + Rules shape established by `prd-from-discussion` / `standup-summary` / `design-review-feedback`. Descriptions lead with trigger phrases for progressive-disclosure name-match. Skills authored:
  - **Designer — `design-handoff-spec`**: Figma frame → engineer-facing handoff with Frame / Layout / Spacing / Typography / Colors / States / Interactions / Assets / Open-questions sections. Grounds every number in the fetched canvas (uses Figma MCP `get_figma_data`); flags WCAG AA contrast failures against the background each color sits on; prefers token names over raw hex when the file uses design tokens.
  - **Engineer — `scope-estimate`**: ticket / spec / spoken ask → T-shirt size (XS = <1h, S = half-day, M = day-or-two, L = week, XL = "break this up") + concrete files-to-touch + blockers + risks + unknowns. No code; no MCP dep. Conservative sizing with explicit calibration. "Name files, not layers" rule prevents the "it's an auth-layer change" kind of non-estimate.
  - **Engineer — `pr-review`**: GitHub PR URL → Summary + Bugs (cited file:line) + Missing-tests + Risks + Style + Questions. Fetches PR via `pull_request_read` + `get_file_contents`. Leads with bugs; does not approve or request changes (just reviews); respects PR intent ("quick fix, full refactor later" → don't critique lack of refactor).
  - **Engineer — `live-bug-triage`**: Sentry + optional claude-code. Five-phase output posted as separate chat messages so the team can redirect mid-triage: (1) what's happening, (2) where it's breaking + stack frame + Sentry link, (3) probable cause with "guess" vs "confirmed" label, (4) proposed fix + file, (5) opt-in "Want me to spin up a claude-code worktree?". Grounds every claim in the Sentry payload; explicitly flags one-off events (count=1 + first=last) as "not a live bug — normal triage."
  - **Engineer — `release-notes`**: GitHub commit range → grouped changelog (Features / Fixes / Changes / Internal) with `#<PR>` links, breaking changes leading with "**BREAKING**". Drops merge commits / version bumps / typo fixes by default. Cites the exact commit range up front as a contract.
  - **PM — `schedule-followup`**: Calendar MCP. Two-phase flow: propose invite (title / when / duration / attendees / calendar / description with artifact URL) → confirm → create → report with event URL. Absolute dates always (convert "Tuesday" → "2026-04-29" using meeting date as anchor). Attendee emails or flag `(need email)` — never guess domain.
- **Engineer skills dir bootstrapped.** Engineer had no `skills/` directory before this commit. Created `src/brainchild/agents/engineer/skills/` and added `agents/engineer/skills` under `skills.paths` in engineer/config.yaml (last-wins override — user skills first, bundle second, matching PM and Designer). Updated the `# Skills —` header comment in engineer/config.yaml to match the bundled-plus-user phrasing from PM/Designer. **Only** engineer config line change in this commit (mcp_servers already landed in 15.7.5).
- **Nine bundled skills now load cleanly** via the real `pipeline/skills.py:load_skills()` path. PM: prd-from-discussion + schedule-followup + standup-summary. Engineer: live-bug-triage + pr-review + release-notes + scope-estimate. Designer: design-handoff-spec + design-review-feedback. Frontmatter validated via `yaml.safe_load` on every file — all nine have valid `name:` + `description:` (description lengths 119–197c). 8/8 test_skills.py + 3/3 test_chat_hardening.py regression-clean.
- **Split-commit rationale**: 15.7.5 and 15.7.6 land as separate commits per user guidance so the phase boundaries are legible in `git log`. Three of 15.7.6's skills (pr-review, release-notes, scope-estimate) are pressure-testable today; the other three (live-bug-triage, design-handoff-spec, schedule-followup) depend on 15.7.5-scaffolded MCPs and light up once users auth them. Pressure-test is the 15.7.5 deferred-live-tests entry + a one-turn trigger per skill per agent.
- **Handoff awareness**: the in-flight session 150 wrote `docs/handoff.md` while 15.7.5 was mid-edit — that handoff pre-credits my commit SHAs and treats 15.7.5+15.7.6 as shipped. Kept handoff.md out of this session's commits so the session-level doc layer stays session 150's to own; appended a session-149-async addendum at end-session time.

**Session 149 (April 22, 2026) — Phase 15.7.4 + 15.7.4.5 shipped. Two commits, ~2.75h.**

- **Entered with session 148's handoff queued up** pointing at 15.7.4 wizard credentials status screen + claude-code prereq check. Pre-implementation Q&A settled three scope points: (a) `credentials_url` is the **remediation URL** per MCP block (docs/settings page where the user acquires the token), distinct from 15.7.3's `auth_url` (the OAuth endpoint mcp-remote hashes); (b) readiness helper lives in new `pipeline/readiness.py` rather than extending `mcp_client.py` because the wizard must import it before `BRAINCHILD_BOT` is set and mcp_client pulls `config` at module-load; (c) the claude-code auth probe uses `claude auth status --json` which returns `{"loggedIn": true/false, ...}` with a clean 0 exit (verified live against the user's machine).
- **Config schema extension.** Added `credentials_url` to all 15 bundled MCP blocks (pm/engineer/designer × claude-code/figma/github/linear/notion). URLs: claude-code docs → `docs.claude.com/en/docs/claude-code/overview`; figma PAT → `figma.com/developers/api#access-tokens`; github token → `github.com/settings/tokens`; linear (OAuth, informational) → `linear.app/settings/account/security`; notion → `notion.so/profile/integrations`. `config.py` passes `credentials_url` through to `MCP_SERVERS` so the runtime pre-flight sees it too.
- **Shared module split.** Extracted `_oauth_cache_exists` + `_mcp_remote_cache_dir` from `mcp_client.py` into new `pipeline/oauth_cache.py` — same code, new location, because the wizard can't import mcp_client (module-level `from brainchild import config` triggers `BRAINCHILD_BOT`-gated load). Also extracted `_run_auth` + `_find_oauth_mcp_config` from `__main__.py` into `pipeline/auth.py` so the wizard's inline "Authorize now?" prompt and the CLI's `brainchild auth <mcp>` share one code path. `__main__.py` re-exports for backward compat; test patch targets for `Path.home` redirected from `mcp_client` to `oauth_cache`.
- **15.7.4 wizard readiness (commit `0432bad`).** New `report_mcp_readiness(mcp_servers) → {name: {status, fix, fix_url, ...}}` returns one of four statuses: `ok`, `missing_env` (with `missing_vars` list), `oauth_needed` (with `auth_url`), `prereq_missing`. Env branch honors pre-resolved `missing_vars` when present (runtime shape) or scans `${VAR}` refs directly (wizard shape — `load_dotenv(override=False)` at module import keeps both paths seeing the same secrets). Claude-code branch: `shutil.which("git")` + `shutil.which("claude")` + `claude auth status --json`, 5s timeout with graceful fallback to `prereq_missing` on every failure mode (timeout, non-zero exit, malformed JSON, `loggedIn: false`). `check_claude_code_auth=False` knob skips the subprocess for callers that want binary-only validation. Wizard `_step2_mcps` now renders `✓/⚠/✗` after the MCP toggle picker, with per-server fix hints + credentials URLs; OAuth-needed servers get an inline "Authorize X now? [Y/n]" loop that calls `run_auth(name)` and re-renders; claude-code in the enabled report triggers a one-liner git-init reminder below the status table. Mid-meeting `delegate_to_claude_code` against a non-git path now says `"Run `git init` in that folder (or point at a folder that's already a git repo) and retry"` instead of the bare "no .git found" message. 20 new tests in `test_1574_readiness.py`.
- **15.7.4.5 runtime pre-flight (commit `a97d4fc`).** `preflight_mcp_readiness(mcp_servers)` in `_run_bot()` after `BRAINCHILD_BOT` is set but before `_run_macos`/`_run_linux` — one platform-agnostic call site. All-ok returns `PREFLIGHT_OK=0` silently (zero visible cost on the happy path). Prompts only when problems exist: oauth_needed default N (auth-now opt-in; mcp-remote takes the terminal + opens browser, not default); missing_env default Y but `n` returns `PREFLIGHT_USER_ABORT=2` so the user can edit `.env` without Ctrl+C mid-join; prereq_missing default Y (claude-code may not even be used this meeting). Uses `check_claude_code_auth=False` — the 5s auth probe is wizard-time only; the 15.7.2 mid-meeting banner catches stale-login with cleaner UX. `EOFError` on `input()` falls back to default so piped / redirected-stdin CI launches don't hang. `--no-preflight` flag bypasses entirely. Helper is `input_fn` / `output_fn` / `run_auth_fn` injectable — 11 new tests in `test_15745_preflight.py` + 2 new in `test_entry_cli.py` cover every status + abort path + EOF fallback + multi-server ordering + `--no-preflight` bypass + `PREFLIGHT_USER_ABORT` short-circuit before dispatch.
- **Regression clean.** 142/142 across 1571 + 1573 + 1574 + 15745 + mcp_client + mcp_shutdown + entry_cli + chat_hardening + 911 + guardrails.
- **Deferred live-smoke entries added** to `docs/deferred-live-tests.md`: (i) wizard readiness UX (happy path + env-missing + OAuth-missing + prereq-missing + inline y/N branches); (ii) claude-code git-init graceful failure (point at `/tmp/not-a-repo` and verify the bot relays the fix message without stack trace); (iii) runtime pre-flight (silent happy path + OAuth-needed inline y/N + missing-env y/n + `--no-preflight` bypass).
- **Exact next step: Phase 15.7.5 new-MCP scaffolding** (~2-3h). Add slack / salesforce / sentry / playwright / google-calendar blocks across all three bundled agents. Default-enablement rule (session 147): an MCP is `enabled: true` on an agent iff a bundled skill on that agent requires it — PM → Linear ✓ + Calendar ✓, Designer → Figma ✓, Engineer → GitHub ✓ + Sentry ✓ + claude-code ✓, Slack/Salesforce/Playwright → scaffolded but `enabled: false` everywhere. Each new block needs `auth` / `credentials_url` / `env` / `read_tools` / `confirm_tools` / `hints`. Run `tests/probe_auth_errors.py` against each with a bogus credential and append captured strings to `docs/mcp-auth-errors.md` + `_AUTH_ERROR_PATTERNS`. Then 15.7.6 six new skills (~2-3h) → 15.8 CLI verb rename (~1.5h) → 14.5 install.sh.

**Planning addition (session 149, April 22, 2026) — Phase 15.8 CLI verb rename added. Docs-only, no code changes.**

- **User raised a CLI UX concern**: `brainchild <name> [url]` isn't action-oriented and collapses the "agents are brainchildren of the user" metaphor — reads as "brainchild, meet pm" (peer-to-peer introduction) rather than a directive to the brainchild system. Walked through alternative verbs.
- **Verbs considered**: `run`, `send`, `meet`, `call`, `summon`, `join`, `launch`. Rejected `meet` + `join` because relational verbs imply two peers meeting each other, which defeats the purpose. `summon` fit the roster / fighter-select metaphor already in the startup banner but felt cute for a CLI. `send` worked for Meet dispatch but got awkward in the no-URL auto-open-meet.new case. Landed on **`run`** — neutral developer vocabulary (matches `docker run`, `npm run`), platform-agnostic, keeps `try` / `setup` / `auth` reading as parallel verbs in the command table.
- **Dropping the package name from the command considered and rejected**. OSS convention isn't "package name must lead" (`ssh host`, `black`, `prettier` all skip it) but "there must be one anchor users can grep shell history, docs, and Google for." Dynamic agent names (`pm`, `engineer`, `designer`) would collide with generic shell vocabulary if installed as loose per-agent binaries; keeping `brainchild` as the anchor preserves discoverability.
- **Phase 15.8 added to `docs/roadmap.md`** between 15.7 and 16. Sequenced **before 14.5 `install.sh`** so the installer's "what's next" message, the README quickstart, and the wizard reveal all ship with the new form in one pass — avoids a follow-up doc sweep a phase later. Two sub-steps: 15.8.0 audit (~30m, inventory every user-facing surface that echoes the bare form — dispatcher + usage string + tests + README + CLAUDE.md + agents README + wizard copy + `ui.say` hints + Linux-adapter help block + doc examples + docstrings) + 15.8.1 rename (~1h, atomic change across all audited surfaces; no dual-accept — bare `brainchild pm` hard-fails with a hint, cleaner failure mode than a transition period where both forms work).
- **Budget impact**: +1.5h on top of the ~6–8h remaining for 15.7. MVP budget moves 28–30h → 29.5–31.5h remaining. Launch target unchanged (Apr 28–30 aspirational, May 1–2 acceptable) — 15.8 is cheap enough to absorb without sliding the window.
- **15.8.0 audit ran in-session** — 21 required changes across 7 files. Breakdown: `__main__.py` (7 hits — module docstring, `_print_usage`, two `ui.say("Restart with:")` hints, `_run_linux` help block); `README.md` (2); `CLAUDE.md` (3 — lines 14–15 Run section + one prose reference at line 87); `src/brainchild/agents/README.md` (2); per-agent READMEs pm/engineer/designer (6, two each); `pipeline/setup.py` (2 — wizard reveal + startup hint); `config.py` (1 — `BRAINCHILD_BOT` missing-env error). **Zero test updates needed** — `tests/test_entry_cli.py` only asserts on subcommand paths (`try` / `auth` / `setup` — all unchanged); `tests/test_setup.py` mocks dispatch. 14 `brainchild try` / `brainchild auth` / `brainchild setup` references across the codebase are unaffected. Full file:line checklist in `docs/roadmap.md` under 15.8.0 — copy-paste-ready for the 15.8.1 implementer. Status stays ⬜ until the 15.8.1 commit ships.
- **Exact next step**: Phase 15.7.4 (wizard credentials status screen + claude-code prereq check, ~2h) per session 148's handoff — unchanged. 15.8 lands after 15.7 closes.

**Session 148 (April 22, 2026) — Phase 15.7.1 + 15.7.2 + 15.7.3 shipped. Three commits, ~5h.**

- **Entered with session 147 planning complete** and the exact next step queued in the handoff: Phase 15.7.1 error classification foundation. Read the scope in `docs/handoff.md` + CLAUDE.md, agreed to proceed.
- **Pre-implementation Q&A** settled three scope choices that shaped the commits: (1) rename `failed_servers` → `startup_failures` + `disabled_servers` → `runtime_failures` instead of just changing their value types — Python's dynamic typing means a pure type change would silently stringify dicts into existing log calls; renaming forces AttributeError on first access so every consumer surfaces at once; (2) 15.7.1 scope stays tight — structured `missing_vars` is the only proactive signal; a real "health probe" upfront (calling a known read tool on each server post-handshake) was rejected as too aggressive for boot time (Playwright-style MCPs spin up browsers on first call); (3) runtime 401/403 sniffing is fuzzy because the MCP spec never defined a semantic error taxonomy — each server just bubbles upstream HTTP errors as free-form strings. Minimal sniff accepted as a deliberate tradeoff with LLM-verbatim relay as the safety net for missed patterns.
- **Empirical auth-error capture (15.7.1a)** — wrote `tests/probe_auth_errors.py` and ran it against the three currently-bundled MCPs with deliberately-bogus tokens. Captured: GitHub `failed to get user: GET https://api.github.com/user: 401 Bad credentials []`; Figma `Error fetching file: Figma API returned 403 Forbidden for '/files/...'`. **Key surprise finding**: Linear via `mcp-remote` does NOT return a 401 on tool call — stdio `initialize()` stalls indefinitely while mcp-remote opens the browser for OAuth. User clicking Cancel on the OAuth popup produced the same stall (confirmed by re-running the probe). **OAuth-over-mcp-remote servers have no sniffable auth-error string.** This reshaped the 15.7.1d sniff list (API-key MCPs only) AND confirmed 15.7.3's cache-path check as the only real signal for OAuth MCPs. Archived findings in `docs/mcp-auth-errors.md` for 15.7.5 MCP additions to re-run.
- **15.7.1 structured classification (commit `6beff98`)** — `_resolve_env_vars` returns `(resolved, missing_vars)` persisted on each server block; `_classify_startup_failure` returns `{kind, fix, raw, [vars]}` with `missing_creds` precedence over whatever stdio raised (the missing secret is almost always the root cause even if the binary crashes with something noisier on top); renamed both failure dicts and flipped their value types to `dict[str, dict]`; `_AUTH_ERROR_PATTERNS` + `_looks_like_auth_error` grounded in empirical captures plus documented patterns (`401`/`403`, `bad credentials`, `forbidden`, `unauthorized`, `invalid_auth`/`not_authed`/`token_expired` for Slack, `invalid_session_id` for Salesforce, `UNAUTHENTICATED`/`invalid_grant` for Google). `record_tool_result` now accepts `error_text` and maintains a `_auth_error_seen` set — if any sub-threshold failure on a server matched an auth pattern, the final trip tags `kind="auth_failed"` instead of `runtime_failure`. 13 new tests in `test_1571_error_classification.py`.
- **15.7.2 proactive banner (commit `43dae3f`)** — `ChatRunner._post_mcp_failure_banner` posts one compact line in `run()` **before** the async intro thread so the banner lands deterministically even if intro generation errors. Label dispatch per `kind`: `missing_creds` inlines the var name for the single-var case ("missing SLACK_BOT_TOKEN") and falls back to generic "credentials" for multi-var; other kinds have short static labels. Multi-failure joins with "; " and closes "Ask for details." Silent on the happy path. Intentionally independent of INTRO_ON_JOIN — failure notice is actionable info the user likely wants even with quiet-bot aesthetic. 6 new tests.
- **15.7.3 OAuth decoupling (commit `ed63026`)** — new `auth: env \| oauth` field + `auth_url` on MCP blocks. `_mcp_remote_cache_dir()` globs `~/.mcp-auth/mcp-remote-*/` and picks lex-latest (so a locally-upgraded mcp-remote doesn't read stale tokens). `_oauth_cache_exists(auth_url)` checks `<md5(auth_url)>_tokens.json` — hashing mirrors mcp-remote's internal `getServerUrlHash` which is `md5(serverUrl)` for the no-headers/no-authorize_resource happy path (confirmed by reading `dist/chunk-*.js` at `~/.npm/_npx/.../mcp-remote/dist/`). Pre-check runs in `connect_all` BEFORE any subprocess spawn for oauth servers — missing cache → skip spawn and record `kind=oauth_needed` with fix pointing at `brainchild auth <name>`. New CLI subcommand foreground-spawns the configured command+args with stdin piped (mcp-remote exits on EOF — pipe keeps it open) and stdout/stderr inherited (user sees the OAuth URL), polls `~/.mcp-auth` for the expected tokens file, SIGTERMs cleanly on appearance. Bundled Linear blocks across all 3 agents declare `auth: oauth` + `auth_url: https://mcp.linear.app/mcp`. **User-owned `~/.brainchild/agents/` intentionally NOT modified** — preserves session 147's insulation promise. 10 new tests in `test_1573_oauth_cache_check.py` + 3 CLI dispatch tests in `test_entry_cli.py`.
- **Deferred-live-tests tracker** — new `docs/deferred-live-tests.md` as a cumulative punch list for smoke tests that need real Meet/browser/LLM roundtrips. Seeded with 15.7.2's banner pressure-test and 15.7.3's full OAuth round-trip (delete cache → confirm banner → run `brainchild auth linear` → cache regenerates → next launch works). Expected to get picked up during Phase 14.8 clean-mac smoke and 15.1 Linux smoke.
- **User raised two expansion ideas at end-of-session** that reshaped 15.7.4 scope forward:
  - **(i) Claude Code MCP prereqs.** claude-code requires git installed + claude CLI installed + claude authed. Forcing these into `install.sh` is wrong (not everyone uses claude-code). Right answer: wizard-time check only when user enables claude-code; probe `shutil.which("git")` + `shutil.which("claude")` + a claude-is-authed check (skip if user says "later"); git-init isn't a pre-req for enablement (per-call concern, MCP takes `repo_path` at invocation). **Folded into 15.7.4 scope** — status screen reports claude-code prereqs alongside other MCP readiness.
  - **(ii) Runtime MCP pre-flight.** If a user hand-edits `~/.brainchild/agents/<name>/config.yaml` to enable an OAuth MCP outside the wizard, 15.7.3's banner catches it mid-meeting — obtrusive. Better: same readiness check runs in `_run_bot()` BEFORE browser spin-up; missing OAuth → interactive "Run auth now? (y/N)" prompt that invokes same code path as `brainchild auth <mcp>` inline. **Split out as new 15.7.4.5** (~45m). Both layers share a `_report_mcp_readiness(mcp_servers)` helper. Belt-and-suspenders vs single-layer wizard-only.
- **Exact next step: Phase 15.7.4 wizard credentials status screen + claude-code prereq check** (~2h, scope expanded from 1.5h with the claude-code gate). Touchpoints: (1) add `credentials_url` field to every bundled MCP block; (2) new `_report_mcp_readiness(mcp_servers) → {mcp_name: {status: "ok|missing|oauth_needed|prereq_missing", fix_url: "..."}}` helper in shared module (candidate: `pipeline/readiness.py` new file, or add to `pipeline/mcp_client.py`); (3) `pipeline/setup.py` end-of-MCP-step status screen using the helper; (4) optional inline OAuth walkthrough that calls into `__main__._run_auth(mcp_name)` directly (requires pulling that out into a plain function callable from the wizard); (5) claude-code-specific prereq branch. Then 15.7.4.5 uses the same helper in `_run_bot()`.
- **Context budget note.** Session 148 burned ~5h of the ~9–11h Phase 15.7 envelope (15.7.1 + 15.7.2 + 15.7.3). Remaining ~6–8h across 15.7.4 / 15.7.4.5 / 15.7.5 / 15.7.6. Launch target unchanged: Apr 28–30 aspirational, May 1–2 acceptable.

**Previous (session 147, April 22, 2026) — docs-only planning session, no code changes.**

- **Entered with session 146 just closed** (`d658b67` doc sync for wizard UX polish + claude-code rename) and the parallel-async working-tree dirt from the session-146 rename audit still visible but owned by another session — left untouched.
- **User opened with a product-shape question** rather than picking up 14.5: the shipped roster has three agents but only three bundled skills (PM has two, Designer has one, Engineer has zero). Wanted 5–10 candidate skills across Designer + Engineer to make the roster feel like a "complete team" — each skill should be mind-reader ("oh cool, didn't realize I could do that") or showcase ("that thing I always prompt my agent for is now a command"). Target persona includes remote teams with AI in meetings, not just solo founders.
- **First-pass skill catalog** drew on existing MCP capabilities only (read-only Figma, GitHub, claude-code, Linear). Proposed `design-handoff-spec` + `accessibility-check` for Designer; `scope-estimate` + `pr-review` for Engineer; flagged `release-notes`, `ci-diagnose`, `codebase-tour` as B-tier. Recommended arc-closing set of four (design-handoff-spec, accessibility-check, scope-estimate, pr-review) that relay-runs from PRD → handoff → scope → PR across PM/Designer/Engineer.
- **User revealed MCPs can be added freely** — "haven't gotten around to it" — which changed the weighting. Second-pass swapped `accessibility-check` out for `design-qa` (requires Browser MCP — compare deployed URL to Figma frame) and swapped `pr-review` out for `live-bug-triage` (requires Sentry MCP — prod-broken-in-meeting iconic moment). New MCPs proposed: Sentry, Browser/Playwright, Slack, Calendar, optional image-gen. Live-bug-triage became the hero engineer skill.
- **User accepted `release-notes` as a fourth engineer skill** (complements PM's standup-summary — meeting recap vs ship recap).
- **Auth-hardening gap surfaced.** User asked what happens when a user enables MCPs in the wizard without providing auth. Traced the code path: `_resolve_env_vars` (`config.py:117`) logs missing `${VAR}` warnings to `/tmp/brainchild.log` but does nothing with the data; `_classify_startup_failure` (`mcp_client.py:58`) categorizes startup failures but doesn't distinguish "missing creds" from "binary crashed"; `record_tool_result` (`mcp_client.py:159`) counts 3 consecutive failures before disabling but doesn't sniff 401/403 for auth-specific framing; `inject_mcp_status` (`llm.py:144`) tells the LLM about failed servers but only if asked. Net: the bot doesn't crash, but a user who enables 5 MCPs without creds sees silent failures + three burned tool calls per unauthed server before lockout, with no proactive heads-up. Four enhancements proposed: persist missing env vars per server, classify missing-creds as its own failure kind, sniff 401/403 at runtime, post a proactive chat banner at meeting join.
- **OAuth hang risk flagged.** If the wizard enables 3 OAuth-style MCPs and the user launches immediately, each spawns at meeting join with a 30s startup timeout and prints a browser URL to the terminal buried under log lines — brutal UX. Proposed: decouple OAuth from meeting join entirely. Cache-check at startup using `~/.mcp-auth/mcp-remote-<version>/<md5(url)>_tokens.json`; if missing, skip spawn + banner. Standalone `brainchild auth <mcp>` subcommand runs the OAuth flow on explicit user action only. **Cache path verified empirically** against existing `~/.mcp-auth/mcp-remote-0.1.37/fcc436b0d1e0a1ed9a2b15bbd638eb13_tokens.json` — `md5("https://mcp.linear.app/mcp")` equals the directory entry hash. Token refresh handled internally by mcp-remote via stored refresh_token. Bumping mcp-remote version invalidates cached tokens (users re-OAuth) — rare but real caveat.
- **Wizard pre-flight pivoted** from "ask for every API key inline" to "check + direct to the right path." User called the inline-form approach burdensome and proposed a status-screen shape: enable MCPs freely, then render a per-MCP `✓/⚠/✗` checklist at the end of the MCP step with remediation URLs for missing creds. Non-blocking — user continues regardless. For OAuth MCPs, optional inline "authorize Linear now? y/n" walk-through runs `brainchild auth linear` under the hood.
- **Five MCPs locked:** slack, salesforce, sentry, playwright, google-calendar. Six skills locked: design-handoff-spec, scope-estimate, pr-review, live-bug-triage, release-notes, schedule-followup (Designer 1, Engineer 4, PM 1). Salesforce + Playwright ship without paired bundled skills — scaffolded-but-disabled everywhere; users surface them via wizard and add their own skills. Likely v1.1 pairs: `deal-brief` (Salesforce on PM) and `design-qa` (Playwright on Designer).
- **Default-enablement rule locked:** an MCP is `enabled: true` on an agent iff a bundled skill on that agent requires it. Final matrix: **PM** → Linear ✓ + Calendar ✓. **Designer** → Figma ✓. **Engineer** → GitHub ✓ + Sentry ✓ + claude-code ✓. This narrows two currently-shipped defaults — PM loses github, Designer loses linear. User-owned `~/.brainchild/agents/` insulates existing installs; only fresh installs see the narrower defaults.
- **Phase 15.7 defined with six sub-phases** (15.7.1 through 15.7.6) and added to `docs/roadmap.md` between 15.6 and 16. Execution order revised: 15.7 sequenced **ahead of 14.5 install.sh** so the installer can seed `~/.brainchild/.env` with the full post-15.7 env-var placeholder set in one pass. MVP budget: 17.5h → 28–30h. Launch target slipped 2 days: Apr 28–30 aspirational, May 1–2 acceptable. Framed as a deliberate launch-quality bet rather than a slip.
- **Session 147 carry-forward questions** (now in 15.7 design notes): non-mcp-remote OAuth paths (v1.1 problem — all five new MCPs are API-key-based), and the scaffolded-but-disabled-skill-less Salesforce + Playwright pairing direction.
- **Next action: Phase 15.7.1 error classification foundation** (~1h). Persist missing env vars from `_resolve_env_vars`, wire into `_classify_startup_failure` with a structured `missing_creds` kind, sniff 401/403 in `record_tool_result`, and propagate richer per-server data through `inject_mcp_status`. Foundation for 15.7.2 banner and 15.7.4 wizard status screen.

**Previous (session 146, April 22, 2026):**

- **Entered with session 145 just closed** (`cd52c0a` doc sync for CLI-surface trim) and a dirty working tree from a parallel-async pass on the setup wizard — session 145's commit-hygiene mishap had unstaged a `delegate_to_claude_code.py → claude_code.py` rename back into the working tree. **Previous (session 144 in progress, April 21, 2026):**

- **Entered session with 14.4 just closed in session 143; user proposed a dep audit before moving on to 14.5.** Goal: walk `requirements.txt` line-by-line and verify every pinned/floored package is actually needed by end users installing via `curl | sh`. Anything not transitively pulled by the 7 direct deps is dead weight on every install.
- **Audit method.** `pipdeptree --reverse` was the first instinct but misses parents that use **extras** (e.g. `pyjwt[crypto]`) — those don't appear in the installed package's `Requires:` metadata field, only in `requires_dist` with an `extra == "..."` marker. Switched to `pip install --dry-run --report report.json` against a clean Python 3.14 venv (throwaway, no voice-pipeline residue) with only the 7 pinned direct deps. The JSON report surfaces every `requires_dist` entry from each resolved package, including extras, so the real parent chain for each transitive became visible.
- **Findings.** Of the 4 `>=` floors: `cryptography` is real (parent chain `mcp → pyjwt[crypto] → cryptography` — the `[crypto]` extra in `mcp==1.27.0`'s `pyjwt[crypto]>=2.10.1` requirement forces it); `pygments` is real (`rich → pygments`); `python-multipart` is real (`mcp → python-multipart`); **`requests` was NOT in the resolved tree at all**. The session-138 `pip-audit` flag came from residual voice-pipeline packages (`elevenlabs`, `spacy`, `google-api-core`) plus dev tools (`pip-audit` itself, `twine`) polluting the audit venv — all transitively use `requests`, none ship to end users. Also spotted that the `# via google-auth` comment on `cryptography` was a stale leftover from the voice era — real parent is `pyjwt[crypto]`.
- **Commit `e1e1c0d` shipped.** Two-line change: dropped `requests>=2.33.0` from `requirements.txt` and `pyproject.toml`; corrected the cryptography comment to reflect the real parent chain. Re-verified end-to-end by rebuilding the wheel from the updated `pyproject.toml`, installing into a second clean venv, and confirming `requests` is absent, `cryptography` still lands, and `brainchild list` works (first-run auto-copy triggers, three bundled agents listed). All 9 canonical test files in CLAUDE.md pass.
- **Next action: Phase 14.5 `install.sh`** (~2h) — bash install script at repo root. Scope unchanged from session 143's handoff: (1) detect macOS/Linux + Python ≥3.10; (2) bootstrap `uv` if missing; (3) `uv tool install git+https://github.com/.../brainchild.git` (blocked on GitHub repo rename `operator → brainchild`); (4) `playwright install chromium` (~170MB); (5) seed `~/.brainchild/.env` with commented API-key placeholders; (6) verify `brainchild` on PATH; (7) print "what's next" pointing at `brainchild setup`. The `.env` priority-ordered resolution (CWD → `~/.brainchild/.env` → shell env) still wants to ship as a 14.4.5 side-commit before 14.5, so the installer can assume the target path is read.
